search_filter_prios = {
	FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL = 1010
	FOCUS_FILTER_RESEARCH = 522
	FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY = 509
	FOCUS_FILTER_SOV_POLITICAL_PARANOIA = 111
	FOCUS_FILTER_PROPAGANDA = 110
	FOCUS_FILTER_ARMY_XP = 103
	FOCUS_FILTER_NAVY_XP = 102
	FOCUS_FILTER_AIR_XP = 101
}

focus_tree = {
	id = generic_focus
	
	country = {
		factor = 1
	}
	
	default = yes
	reset_on_civilwar = no

	initial_show_position = {
		focus = generic_army_effort
	}



	focus = {
		id = generic_army_effort
		icon = GFX_goal_generic_allies_build_infantry
		x = 0
		y = 0
		cost = 5
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ARMY_XP FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }
		
		available_if_capitulated = yes

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				date < 1937.1.1				
			}			
		}

		completion_reward = {
			army_experience = 10
			add_doctrine_cost_reduction = {
				name = land_doc_bonus
				cost_reduction = 0.25
				uses = 1
				category = land_doctrine
			}
		}
		complete_tooltip = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}

		completion_reward = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_owned_state = {
						free_building_slots = {
							building = arms_factory
							size > 0
							include_locked = yes
						}
					}
				}
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						free_building_slots = {
							building = arms_factory
							size > 0
							include_locked = yes
						}
					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					add_building_construction = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						any_owned_state = {
							free_building_slots = {
								building = arms_factory
								size > 0
								include_locked = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
				random_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						free_building_slots = {
							building = arms_factory
							size > 0
							include_locked = yes
						}
					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					add_building_construction = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
			}			
		}
	}

			}
		}
		complete_tooltip = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}

		completion_reward = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_owned_state = {
						free_building_slots = {
							building = arms_factory
							size > 0
							include_locked = yes
						}
					}
				}
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						free_building_slots = {
							building = arms_factory
							size > 0
							include_locked = yes
						}
					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					add_building_construction = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						any_owned_state = {
							free_building_slots = {
								building = arms_factory
								size > 0
								include_locked = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
				random_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						free_building_slots = {
							building = arms_factory
							size > 0
							include_locked = yes
						}
					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					add_building_construction = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
			}			
		}
		completion_reward = {
			add_offsite_building = { type = arms_factory level = 1 }
		}		
	}
